  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(document).ready(function() {
 
	var watermark = 'Search PlayStation Forums';
 
	//init, set watermark text and class
	$('#messageSearchField').val(watermark).addClass('watermark');
 
	//if blur and no value inside, set watermark text and class again.
 	$('#messageSearchField').blur(function(){
  		if ($(this).val().length == 0){
    		$(this).val(watermark).addClass('watermark');
		}
 	});
 
	//if focus and text is watermrk, set it to empty and remove the watermark class
	$('#messageSearchField').focus(function(){
  		if ($(this).val() == watermark){
    		$(this).val('').removeClass('watermark');
		}
 	});
});
  </script>

   $(document).ready(function(){
  $("#submitContext").click(function(){
   trackSearch.call(this);
  });
  
   $('.lia-autocomplete-container').mouseup(function() {
  trackSearch.call(this);

function trackSearch() {
 var searchTxt = $('.lia-form-type-text.lia-autocomplete-input.search-input.lia-search-input-message').val();
 ClickOmniSearch(this, 'event17', 'search', searchTxt, $(this).find('a').eq(1).text());
}

function ClickOmniSearch(obj, eventVal, secName, valueToSearch, sugValue) {
 secName = secName + ":" + pageName;
 s.events = eventVal;
 s.linkTrackEvents = eventVal;
 s.eVar17 = s.prop17 = valueToSearch;
 s.eVar18 = s.prop18 = sugValue || '';
 s.linkTrackVars = 'prop17,eVar17,events,eVar18,prop18';
 s.pageName = secName;
 s.tl(obj, 'o', secName);
}
function searchCal()
{
}

   ;( function( $, undefined )
{
    $.fn.UserNotifications = function()
    {
        var $item   = $( '#user-notifications-menu-top' )
          , $list   = $item.find( '#notification-list' )
          , unread  = parseInt( $item.find( '.user-navigation-combine-notification-feed .lia-header-nav-component-unread-count' ).text() )
          , pageURL = $item.find( '.user-navigation-combine-notification-feed .lia-link-navigation' ).attr( 'href' );

        $item.find( '#alerts-count' ).text( unread );
        $item.find( '#notifications-page-link' ).attr( 'href', pageURL );

        if( unread &gt; 0 )
        {
            $item.addClass( 'new-notifications' );
            $("#user-notifications-menu-top #notification-list &gt; li:lt("+unread+")").addClass("unread");
        }
        else
        {
            $item.addClass( 'no-new-notifications' );
        }
    };

} )( jQuery );
  </script>

     var jquery_1_7_2 = $;

$(document).ready(function() {
     if(!$("#lia-body").hasClass("SearchPage")) {
          $("#lia-searchform").appendTo(".main-sub-nav .sub-nav-link-container");
     }
     if($(".lia-message-board").hasClass("lia-panel-message-root")) {
          $(".ForumTopicPage #pager").appendTo(".lia-panel-message-root");
     }
     if($(".threaded-message-list #messageview .lia-message-board").hasClass("lia-panel-message")) {
          $(".ForumTopicPage .lia-menu-bar-top.top-block").appendTo("#messageview .lia-panel-message");
     }
	else if($("#lineardisplaymessageviewwrapper .lia-message-board").hasClass("lia-panel-message-root")) {
          $(".ForumTopicPage .lia-menu-bar-top.top-block").appendTo(".lia-panel-message-root");
     }

     

     if($(".lia-message-board").hasClass("lia-panel-message-root")) {
          $(".ForumTopicPage #messageview .InfoMessage").appendTo("#lia-body.ForumTopicPage .lia-content #messageview .lia-panel-message-root .lia-quilt-row-forum-message-main &gt; .lia-quilt-column-main-right");
          //$(".lia-panel-message-root").prepend($(".ForumTopicPage #messageview .InfoMessage"));
     }

				$.fn.scrollBottom = function() {
					return $(document).height() - this.scrollTop() - this.height();
				};

				var $el = $('.main-sub-nav');
				var $window = $(window);
				$window.bind("scroll resize load", function() {
					$('.main-sub-nav').show();
					var gap = $window.height() - $el.height() - 10;
					var visibleFoot = 62 - $window.scrollBottom();
					var scrollTop = $window.scrollTop()
					
					if(scrollTop &lt; 62 + 10){
						$el.css({
							top: (62 - scrollTop) + "px",
							bottom: "auto", background: "transparent"
						});
					} else {
						$el.css({
							top: 0,
							bottom: "auto",background: "#363636"
						});
					}
				});
			});

                                          <a class="lia-link-navigation report-abuse-link lia-component-forums-action-report-abuse" href="/t5/notifications/notifymoderatorpage/message-uid/42133811" id="reportAbuse">

                              <div class="thread-details">
                               <span class="replies">
                                <strong>
                                 1575
                                </strong>
                                replies
                               </span>
                               <span class="views">
                                <strong>
                                 194089
                                </strong>
                                views
                               </span>
                               <span class="edit">
                                Edited
                                <strong>
                                 Sep 11, 2014
                                </strong>
                               </span>
                              </div>
                              <div class="lia-message-body" id="messagebodydisplay">
                               <div class="lia-message-body-content">
                                <p>
                                 <span>
                                  Hello PlayStation Community,
                                 </span>
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                 <span>
                                 </span>
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                 <span>
                                  We have noticed various reports of users having trouble ejecting PS4 discs.
                                 </span>
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                 <span>
                                  Update: Pleases refer toour troubleshooting video for disc ejection issues first.
                                 </span>
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                 <span>
                                  <div class="video-embed-center video-embed-youtube">
                                   <iframe allowfullscreen="true" frameborder="0" height="265" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/yU2Z6alUAcI" width="320">
                                   </iframe>
                                  </div>
                                 </span>
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                 <span>
                                  If you are experiencing this issue or a similar case, please share the following information below:
                                 </span>
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                 <span>
                                 </span>
                                </p>
                                <ul>
                                 <li>
                                  What title were you trying to eject?
                                 </li>
                                 <li>
                                  Were you installing any game data at the time?
                                 </li>
                                 <li>
                                  Did you see any game or system notifications beforehand (Ready to install notifications, error messages, etc.)?
                                 </li>
                                 <li>
                                  What troubleshooting steps did you attempt?
                                 </li>
                                </ul>
                                <p>
                                 If you are currently trying to remove a disk in your PS4, you can use the manual ejection method listed here:
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                 <a href="https://support.us.playstation.com/app/answers/detail/a_id/5061/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                                  https://support.us.playstation.com/app/answers/det
                                  <wbr>
                                  </wbr>
                                  ail/a_id/5061/
                                 </a>
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                 <span style="text-decoration: underline;">
                                  <strong>
                                   If you are encountering the specific issue where your game crashes in the middle of gameplay and your disc is no longer recognized, here are a few things to try:
                                  </strong>
                                 </span>
                                </p>
                                <ul>
                                 <li>
                                  You can try deleting the specific game app data and reinstalling
                                 </li>
                                 <li>
                                  If your save data is corrupt, you can try deleting it
                                 </li>
                                 <li>
                                  There are a number of PS4 safe mode options that may help as well.
                                 </li>
                                </ul>
                                <p>
                                 <a href="https://support.us.playstation.com/app/answers/detail/a_id/5044" rel="nofollow" style="font-size: 12px;" target="_blank">
                                  https://support.us.playstation.com/app/answers/det
                                  <wbr>
                                  </wbr>
                                  ail/a_id/5044
                                 </a>
                                 <br/>
                                 <em style="font-size: 12px;">
                                  <strong>
                                   (Notice: If updating firmware by USB, make sure the flash drive is formatted for FAT32)
                                  </strong>
                                 </em>
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                 <span style="font-size: 12px;">
                                  The following options are available in Safe Mode:
                                 </span>
                                </p>
                                <ol>
                                 <li>
                                  Restart System- Ends Safe Mode and restarts the PlayStation 4 normally.
                                 </li>
                                 <li>
                                  <span>
                                   Change Resolution- Changes the screen resolution to 480p when the PlayStation 4 is restarted.
                                  </span>
                                 </li>
                                 <li>
                                  <span>
                                   Update System Software- Allows the PlayStation 4 to update the system software via Internet, USB Drive, or Disc.
                                  </span>
                                 </li>
                                 <li>
                                  <span>
                                   Restore Default Settings- Restores the PlayStation 4 to the default factory settings.
                                  </span>
                                 </li>
                                 <li>
                                  <span>
                                   Rebuild Database- Scans the drive and creates a new database of all content.
                                  </span>
                                  This operation may take a long time depending on the type and number of data items.
                                 </li>
                                 <li>
                                  <span>
                                   Initialize PS4-
                                  </span>
                                  <span class="kc-warning">
                                   IMPORTANT
                                  </span>
                                  <span>
                                   : All data and settings will be lost by performing this step.
                                  </span>
                                  Deletes all user data and restores the PS4 to as if it just came out of the box. This option is the same as [Initialize PS4 ] in the (Settings) menu. System software (firmware) is not deleted.
                                 </li>
                                 <li>
                                  <span>
                                   Initialize PS4 (Reinstall System Software)-
                                  </span>
                                  <strong class="kc-warning">
                                   IMPORTANT
                                  </strong>
                                  <span>
                                   : Deletes all information on the HDD, including the System Software. A message that states a USB storage device containing the System Software must be connected, is displayed. Then you can confirm the selection. (You will need the full system update installer from
                                   <a href="http://us.playstation.com/support/systemupdates/ps4/pc_update/index.htm" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                                    http://us.playstation.com/support/systemupdates/ps
                                    <wbr>
                                    </wbr>
                                    4/pc_update/index.htm
                                   </a>
                                   with this option)
                                  </span>
                                 </li>
                                </ol>
                                <p>
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                 <span style="text-decoration: underline;">
                                  <strong>
                                   For additional service/replacement options please try contacting support:
                                  </strong>
                                 </span>
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                 <a href="https://support.us.playstation.com/app/contact_options" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                                  https://support.us.playstation.com/app/contact_opt
                                  <wbr>
                                  </wbr>
                                  ions
                                 </a>
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                 Due to the number of contacts, we would suggest using the Live Chat option rather than a phone call as the wait times tend to be shorter.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                 We appreciate your patience while we investigate. Thanks.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                 U--J
                                </p>
                                <div class="UserSignature lia-message-signature">
                                 PlayStation Moderation and Support Guy @ www.playstationsupportforum.com
                                </div>

                               <div class="lia-message-body-content">
                                <p>
                                 That's just great. I did find
                                 <a href="https://support.us.playstation.com/app/answers/detail/a_id/5061/related/1" rel="nofollow" target="_self">

				this.queue = [];

			PDCFunctionQueue.prototype.addToQueue = function(funcItem){

				this.queue.push(funcItem);
			};
			PDCFunctionQueue.prototype.clearQueue = function(){
				this.queue.length = 0;
			};
			PDCFunctionQueue.prototype.executeQueue = function(){

				var nQueueLength = this.queue.length;
				var sTargetID,
					sMethodName,
					aParams,
					$targetElement,
					fMethod;

				for (var i = 0; i &lt; this.queue.length; i++) {
					try {
						var funcItem = this.queue[i];

						if (typeof funcItem === 'object') {

								sTargetID = funcItem['id'];
								sMethodName = funcItem['method'];
								aParams = funcItem['params'];
								$targetElement = $(document.getElementById(sTargetID));
								fMethod = $targetElement[sMethodName];
								fMethod.apply($targetElement, aParams);

						} else if (typeof funcItem === 'string' &amp;&amp; PDC.Func) {

							if (typeof PDC.Func[funcItem] === 'function') {
								PDC.Func[funcItem].call();
							}

						}
						
					} catch(err) {
					
						if (typeof console == "object") {
							console.log("Error running script - " + err + " (Has plugin been included?)");
							console.log({
								"sTargetID" : sTargetID,
								"sMethodName" : sMethodName,
								"aParams" : aParams,
								"$targetElement" : $targetElement,
								"fMethod" : fMethod
							});
							
						}
						
					}
					
				}
				this.clearQueue();
			};
			var PDC = PDC || {};
			PDC.funcQueue = PDC.funcQueue || new PDCFunctionQueue();
         </script>
         <script type="text/javascript">
          PDC.funcQueue.addToQueue('CM066');
         </script>
         <script type="text/javascript">
          PDC.funcQueue.executeQueue();

	function setEventVars(pageName) {
	var pEvents = new Array();// creating an array
	if(map[pageName] != undefined) // page specific variables exists
		pEvents = map[pageName]['events'].split(',');// split the variable seperated by comma and store them in the pEvents array
		
	var events = map['all']['events'].split(',').concat(pEvents); // add page specifc vars to those common to all
	var sEvents = "";
	var eventsSeparator = "";
	var productsSeparator = "";
	var sProducts = ";;;;";
	var event = null;
	
	for (var i in events) {
		if(events[i] != '' &amp;&amp; events.hasOwnProperty(i)) {
			// events is an array, not object
			event = events[i];
			sEvents += eventsSeparator + event; // s.events = 'event90,event92';
			
			if(events_map[event] != null &amp;&amp; events_map[event] != '') {
				// If events are just numerics, don't add to s.products
				
				productsSeparator = "|";
				}
			eventsSeparator = ",";
			}
		}

	s.events = sEvents;
	
	}

function setVarsFromJSON(pageName) {
	var all = map['all']; // variables common to all pages
	for(var key in all) { // set variables common to all pages
		if(key != null &amp;&amp; all.hasOwnProperty(key) &amp;&amp; key != 'events') {
			s[key] = all[key]; //s.prop32, s.eVar33 etc
			}
		}
	
	var custom = map[pageName]; // page specific variables
	for(var customKey in custom) { // set page specific variables
		if(customKey != null &amp;&amp; custom.hasOwnProperty(customKey) &amp;&amp; customKey != 'events') {
			s[customKey] = custom[customKey]; //s.prop32, s.eVar33 etc
			}
		}
	setEventVars(pageName); // separate function to populate event vars as some  might be numeric events
	}
